example of REST API use.\n\n1. To use the REST API, you must first generate the API key required for authenticating API requests. The following\n *cURL* example shows a *GET* request whose response will include the API key.\n\n ```shell\n curl -X GET 'https://YOUR_HOST_URL/api/?type=keygen&user=<username>&password=<password>'\n ```\n\nThe following shows the format of a successful response. The key element contains the API key to specify\nas the value for the HTTP request header *X-PAN-KEY* in subsequent REST API requests.\n\n ```xml\n  <response status = 'success'>\n     <result>\n         <key>YOUR_API_KEY</key>\n     </result>\n  </response>\n```\n\n2. The following *cURL* example shows a REST API request to return a list of predefined tags from the firewall:\n\n```shell\n  curl -X GET https://YOUR_HOST_URL/restapi/v10.0/objects/tags?location=predefined --header 'X-PAN-KEY: YOUR_API_KEY'\n```\n\n  The following is an example of a successful response:\n\n```json\n  {\n    \"@status\": \"success\",\n    \"@code\": \"19\",\n    \"result\": {\n      \"@total-count\": \"2\",\n       \"@count\": \"2\",\n      \"entry\": [\n          {\n            \"@name\": \"Sanctioned\",\n            \"@location\": \"predefined\",\n            \"color\": \"color17\"\n          },\n          {\n            \"@name\": \"empty\",\n            \"@location\": \"predefined\"\n          }\n       ]\n    }\n  }\n```\n"},"postman":{"name":"List Virtal Routers","description":{"content":"Get Virtal Routers.\n","type":"text/plain"},"url":{"path":["restapi","v10.0","VirtualRouters"],"host":["{{baseUrl}}"],"query":[{"disabled":false,"description":{"content":"The name of the entry","type":"text/plain"},"key":"name","value":""},{"disabled":false,"key":"location","value":""},{"disabled":false,"description":{"content":"Specify the output format to be JSON or XML.\nThis is equivalent to setting the `Accept` header to `application/json` or `application/xml`.\nIf you include both `output-format` and `Accept` header, the value of `output-format` will override the header.\n","type":"text/plain"},"key":"output-format","value":""}],"variable":[]},"header":[{"key":"Accept","value":"application/json"}],"method":"GET"}}
